Teodoro The hotel San Teodoro is situated in one of the most funny corners of the east coast of Sardinia a few minutes away from the village of San Teodoro km and close to its famous beaches La Cinta and Cala d Ambra km The Hotel nestled like a gem between the Mediterranean scrub and the crystal clear sea is built in typical Mediterranean style and blends perfectly with the surrounding environment you will find a sheltered relaxation area its secluded position makes this hotel a true oasis of peace and serenity HOTEL Hotel San Teodoro has facilities like a spacious hall a restaurant offering local and international cuisine and a bar with an outdoor area overlooking the wonderful green park with Kids area and dedicated playground The hotel also has an unsupervised parking area and Shuttle Bus service to the famous beaches and San Teodoro village with its shops restaurants and services ROOMS The rooms are furnished with care and are equipped with satellite TV Sky air conditioning telephone Wi fi minibar safe box and have private facilities with shower and hair dryer The rooms are situated on the ground floor with a patio or the first and second floor with balcony two different rooms types Classic and Elegant that can be easily reach by a modern see through lift SERVICES Walking on the green park you can reach a tennis court and the swimming pool where our guests can enjoy free of charge beach umbrellas and sun beds also we can offer excursions and walking routes around the protected Sea area with Tavolara isle I Giardini di Punta Molara Coda Cavallo and Puntaldia or on the hinterlands as Orgosolo Supramonte or Tiscali Village The Hotel has facilities like a spacious hall a restaurant H O offering local and international cuisine and the Mariposa Lounge Bar with an outdoor area overlooking the wonderful green park Rezeptionszeiten Jeden Tag von bis Uhr Daten des Hotels Hotel Baujahr Letzte Gesamt Renovierung Letzte Teil Renovierung Anzahl Etagen Gesamtanzahl beautiful bay of Capo Coda Cavallo recently became the Marine Park strategically located in front of the fabulous islands Tavolara and Molara easily accessible by sea It s situated near the sea which is to meters the beach is also accessible walk through a steep path or by stairs In addition near the residence there are many other great beaches all are within a very short time by the car for example the beautiful beach Calabrandinchi Tahiti just Km Inside the village you can find a swimming pool two bars a restaurant and a pizzeria The market however is in the nearby village of Porto Coda Cavallo in a short distance Extra services are provided by third parties and rent to be paid locally Pets are generally allowed fee but you should be requested when booking ROOMS APARTMENTS
